# Parity Gaps — ranked by gameplay impact

_Generated 2026-06-23. 1080 features with gaps, highest-impact first._

Score weights logic & liveness highest, then values/timing, then presentation/audio, scaled by category (core gameplay > niche entities). Intended divergences excluded.

| # | score | unit | feature | worst | gaps |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | 27.0 | `assault` | `assault.mapobject.assault_wall` | logic:missing | STILL a no-op: func_assault_wall edicts are consumed (GameWorld.cs:1666-1670, then RetirePlaceholder) with no behavior. The wall that should hide (model='' + SOLID_NOT) once its objective is destroyed and reappear otherwise does neither, so a path that QC opens by destroying an objective stays blocked (or vice versa). |
| 2 | 22.5 | `assault` | `assault.round.second_round` | liveness:dead | STILL DEAD: StartSecondRound() has ZERO live callers (grep across src/ tests/ game/ = only doc-comment references inside Assault.cs). DriveFrame is now driven per-frame (DriveGametypeFrame:1817), but nothing flips to round 2 when round 1 is decided — DriveFrame/DestroyFinalObjective record FirstRoundDestroyTime and broadcast OBJ_DESTROYED, then expect a StartSecondRound that never fires. Roles never swap; the faster-destroyer overall winner is never decided.; The 5s AS_ROUND_DELAY freeze (as_round entity nextthink) + ReadyRestart_force map reset + bprint('Starting second round...') + the timelimit bump (autocvar_timelimit + AS_ROUND_DELAY/60) are not implemented.; Round 2's timelimit (= round 1 destruction time) is recorded as FirstRoundDestroyTime and consulted by DriveFrame, but no caller ever sets State.Round=1 so the round-2 branch is unreachable. |
